The minimalist interface hides a number of powerful writing features\r\n\r\nWORDCOUNT TOOLS\r\n===============\r\nSee at a glance how many words are in your document, or how many you've written since you opened the app. \r\n\r\nWORDCOUNT GOAL\r\n==============\r\nSet yourself a target - for example, 500 words - and Poe will let you know when you've reached that goal with a non-intrusive toast notification\r\n\r\nWRITING TIMER\r\n=============\r\nGot a limited amount of time to write? Set yourself an alarm to let you know when it's time to stop writing. Poe saves right back to the file you opened. It also keeps any unsaved work in temp files. If you close the app and forget to save, Poe resurrects your work and prompts you to save it this time. With a 360° view of your business information at your finger-tips, you can stay on top of things when dealing with your customers. \r\n\r\nElegantly Simple\r\nWe use the elegantly simple \"Cards-and-Paper\" metaphor to design our user interface. The \"Cards\" is on the left-hand side of the app to reference a list of customers, inventory items and pricing. You can reference the \"Cards\" to add inventory items onto the \"Paper\" (which is the invoice) on the right. This is a metaphor that most of us, who need to issue invoices, can understand, visualize and associate with. We gleaned this metaphor from previous experiences where we successfully helped fast-growing companies transform their on the go manual \"Cards-and-Paper\" invoice issuance to that of a fully automated one using our software.
